Hygiene: It can be seen that the decoration has been done for many years, and some places of hygiene are not clean.
Environment: The environment is really beautiful, suitable for bringing children to live.
Service: Because we bought a package ticket, including a scenic spot ticket, we originally wanted to go to the amusement park first, fortunately the front desk staff reminded us that it was Monday and there was no big circus performance. In addition, there was a short little girl without glasses in the restaurant who had a very good service attitude, but there were two waiters with glasses who looked fierce. There was a dish for dinner that had not been served. We waited two or three times and asked the waiters with glasses, but they always had an attitude of "wait a minute, it will be served soon". Only this girl came to us and apologized embarrassedly. And the next day at breakfast, because most hotels require room cards to eat breakfast, or go to eat directly, only this hotel still uses paper breakfast coupons, so we forgot to bring them, and my family went back to the room to get them. Then the girl told us to go in first, which was very heartwarming.

At the same time, since it is close to the national 4A-level tourist attraction-Olebo Ocean Polar World, guests can easily visit these tourist spots.
2. **Enthusiastic service**: The hotel has a good service attitude, the staff is warm and welcoming, and can respond to guests' needs in a timely manner.
3. **Satisfactory catering**: The breakfast and dinner provided by the hotel are all buffets, with a variety of varieties and very good taste. You can enjoy grilled squid and crayfish freely.
4. **Suitable for families**: As a parent-child hotel, it has special accommodation facilities such as the Magic Knight House and the Forest Tree House that are loved by families. It is especially suitable for families with children.
5. **Theme features**: The hotel's medieval knight theme design makes people feel like traveling back to ancient times. This unique theme style is great.
6. **Hot spring enjoyment**: The hotel has a health hot spring, which provides tourists with a good place to relax.
7. **High overall score**: The facilities in the house are very creative, including the tree house, jigsaw toiletries, welcome fruits, and the height of the wash basin that many parent-child hotels should emulate. Very nice!

Overall, the Knights Hotel Oleburg, Texas has won praise from many tourists for its unique design and thoughtful service. It is especially suitable for travelers who are looking for a unique accommodation experience and want to spend a good time with their family.
